LU-13139 obdclass: collect stats for OSD methods

frequency and time spent in each method is collected,
then can be found in os[dp].*.osd_stats and lod.*.osd_stats:

osd-ldiskfs.lustre-MDT0000.osd_stats=
snapshot_time             1674142976.044241006 secs.nsecs

trans_stop                259 samples [usecs] 0 1906 11820 10291894

decl_create               100 samples [usecs] 0 12 57 491

xattr_get                 35 samples [usecs] 0 7 17 91

...

--- Message (James Simmons, 2025-02-18 14:34:56.000000000) ---
Patch Set 41: Code-Review-1

Issues with GPL only modules symbols. For the added ktime_* in dt_* inline function in dt_object.h will need to be turned into real function in dt_object.c to avoid the issues. For debugfs_create_file a wrapper will need to written for lprocfs_stats_server.c.

--- Message (Andreas Dilger, 2025-02-18 14:42:19.000000000) ---
Patch Set 41:

James, rather than blocking this ready-to-land patch for a kernel nobody is using yet, I'd rather this land and then the issue be fixed when server support for the new kernel is added.

That could be fixed a variety of ways without dropping ZFS support completely:
- make these stats conditional in ZFS depending on whether ktime_get() is GPL-only
- add a compat function for ktime_get() that reverse engineers the nanoseconds from some time function (eg. ktime_get_time_ts64() or whatever)
- add an optional server kernel patch to change the EXPORT_SYMBOL()
- add a helper function in obdclass

--- Message (Timothy Day, 2025-02-18 15:24:46.000000000) ---
Patch Set 41:

It seems like ktime_get() is EXPORT_SYMBOL_GPL() as far back as 4.20 kernel [1]. But this patch definitely passed ZFS Maloo testing. Do vendor kernels s/EXPORT_SYMBOL/EXPORT_SYMBOL_GPL/g for some symbols? James, what kernel are you using?

[1] https://elixir.bootlin.com/linux/v4.20.17/source/kernel/time/timekeeping.c#L746

--- Message (Andreas Dilger, 2025-02-18 16:03:43.000000000) ---
Patch Set 41:

> It seems like ktime_get() is EXPORT_SYMBOL_GPL() as far back as
 > 4.20 kernel [1]. But this patch definitely passed ZFS Maloo
 > testing. Do vendor kernels s/EXPORT_SYMBOL/EXPORT_SYMBOL_GPL/g for
 > some symbols? James, what kernel are you using?

The WC autotest testing is running on el9.x with ZFS servers, and it is using ktime_get_real_seconds() (EXPORT_SYMBOL_GPL()), but this is the first time ktime_get() is used. 

It may be that newer kernels have become more anal and now the non-GPL module load prevents the module from loading GPL symbols?

I still think this patch should land as-is, because the GPL symbol usage in osd-zfs predates this patch and isn't a reason to not land it.

--- Message (Timothy Day, 2025-02-18 19:16:41.000000000) ---
Patch Set 41:

> It may be that newer kernels have become more anal and now the non-GPL module load prevents the module from loading GPL symbols?

I think that's it. Christoph Hellwig pushed a patch to make module loading more strict. The RHEL kernels must not have that patch.

[1] https://git.kernel.org/pub/scm/linux/kernel/git/torvalds/linux.git/commit/?id=262e6ae7081d
